#Noble families for admin government
#These really should have been county level instead so they didn't mess up the themata but not sure if that'd break anything
#Only worth setting characters for specific dates since I don't think there's any real benefit to doing a line of rulers and filling out the titles screws with the themata if they happen to be landed but not themata rulers as I generally landed the important noble families

# More Bookmarks Noble Families

##Japan - Don't want to script these as I actually want the title history in these. Only doing the major families for 769 to 1185. For the last 3 it's mainly focusing on the branch that was most relevent by 1185. Main reason for this is to have the major families exist politicaly like they should but not use admin government on the regular titles as that doesn't really fit outside 769. I can't find anything like a list of house heads for any of the families outside maybe the period near the Genpei War so it's mostly just going to be picking a random character from these families
##Fujiwara - Oshu, Hokke, Nanke, Shikkike, and Kyoke
##Minamoto
##Taira

## The Fujiwara are broken up into their branch families so going to add each one of them. According to the Japanese wikipedia there was no Nanke, Hokke etc. clan chief and just an overall single person for all the branches (and apparently entirely the Hokke branch by the 800's) but for gameplay purposes it's better to break them up as otherwise whichever family has the noble family title at a bookmark start is always going to hold it while the others will never get one as there's no mechanic for the title bouncing between dynasties
